			// Produces an array with [0] being consent group IDs (ex: ['C0002]) and [1] being GA3 dimensions

			function getGA3Dimensions(activeConsentGroups = []) {
				return ga3ConsentGroupsToDimensions.reduce((acc, [requiredConsents, dimensions]) => {
					const hasRequiredConsents = requiredConsents.every((consent) => activeConsentGroups.includes(consent));
					if (hasRequiredConsents) {
						return {...acc, ...dimensions};
					}
					return acc;
				}, {});
			}

			// Produces an array of GA4 dimensions that can be populated granted the current level of user consent.
			function getGA4Dimensions(activeConsentGroups = []) {
				const ga3Dimensions = getGA3Dimensions(activeConsentGroups);

				return pmc_ga_mapped_dimensions
					? mapGA3DimensionsToGA4(ga3Dimensions, pmc_ga_mapped_dimensions)
					: ga3Dimensions;
			}
		</script>

		<script>
			if ( 'undefined' !== typeof jQuery ) {
				var $pmc_ad_bait = jQuery('#pmc-ad-bait');
				if ( $pmc_ad_bait.length ) {
					if ( 'block' !== $pmc_ad_bait.css('display') ) {

		</script>
		<script>
	/**
	 * Remove all elements with this selector.
	 *
	 * @param selectors Array of selectors.
	 */
	function pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( selectors ) {
		if ( 'object' !== typeof selectors ) {
			return;
		}

		for ( var i = 0; i < selectors.length; i++ ) {
			var element = ( 'li' === selectors[i].parentNode.nodeName.toLowerCase() ) ? selectors[i].parentElement : selectors[i];

			element.remove();
		}
	}

	/**
	 * Toggle clicks of elements with this selector.
	 *
	 * @param selectors Array of selectors.
	 */
	function pmc_onetrust_toggle_clicks( selectors ) {
		if ( 'object' !== typeof selectors || 'object' !== typeof OneTrust ) {
			return;
		}

		for ( var i = 0; i < selectors.length; i++ ) {
			var element = ( 'li' === selectors[i].parentNode.nodeName.toLowerCase() ) ? selectors[i].parentElement : selectors[i];

			element.addEventListener( 'click', function( e ) {
				e.preventDefault();
				OneTrust.ToggleInfoDisplay();
			} );
		}
	}

	/**
	 * Is the user's current region an opt-in region?
	 *
	 * Opt-in regions are those where certain cookie categories are disabled by
	 * default but can be opted into. Example: GDPR
	 *
	 * @return bool
	 */
	function pmc_onetrust_is_opt_in_region() {
		return 'EU' === pmc_fastly_geo_data.continent;
	}

	/**
	 * Is the user's current region an opt-out region?
	 *
	 * Opt-out regions are those where certain cookie categories are enabled by
	 * default but can be opted out of. Examples: California, Virginia.
	 *
	 * @return bool
	 */
	function pmc_onetrust_is_opt_out_region() {
		return [
			'CA',
			'CO',
			'CT',
			'DE',
			'IA',
			'IN',
			'KY',
			'MD',
			'MN',
			'MT',
			'NE',
			'NH',
			'NJ',
			'OR',
			'RI',
			'TN',
			'TX',
			'UT',
			'VA',
		].includes( pmc_fastly_geo_data.region );
	}

	/**
	 * Is the user's current region California?
	 *
	 * @return bool
	 */
	function pmc_onetrust_is_ca() {
		return 'CA' === pmc_fastly_geo_data.region;
	}


	if ( 'object' === typeof pmc_fastly_geo_data ) {
		var optOutLink = document.querySelectorAll( "a[href='https:\/\/pmc.com\/opt-out']" );
		var optInLink = document.querySelectorAll( ".menu-item.privacy-consent" );

		// Only leave CA link for CA visitors.
		if ( ! pmc_onetrust_is_ca() ) {
			pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( document.querySelectorAll(
				"a[href='https:\/\/pmc.com\/privacy-policy\/#california']"			) );
		}

		// CCPA and the like (CA, CO, CT, VA, etc).
		if ( pmc_onetrust_is_opt_out_region() ) {
			pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( optInLink );
			pmc_onetrust_toggle_clicks( optOutLink );

			// GDPR.
		} else if ( pmc_onetrust_is_opt_in_region() ) {
			pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( optOutLink );
			pmc_onetrust_toggle_clicks( optInLink );

			// Everywhere else.
		} else {
			pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( optInLink );
			pmc_onetrust_remove_elements( optOutLink );
		}
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
window.pmc = window.pmc || {};
window.pmc.analytics = window.pmc.analytics || [];

function global_urlhashchanged() {
	/**
	 * Track pageview
	 */
	// Build the current domain name
	var tmp_td = document.domain.split('.');
	var tracking_domain = tmp_td[tmp_td.length-2] + "." + tmp_td[tmp_td.length-1];

	// Build the current image
	var imgname = location.hash.replace('#','');
	try {
		window.pmc.analytics.push(function() {
			window.pmc.analytics.track_pageview( location.pathname + location.hash );
		});
	} catch(err) {}

	try {
		if ( typeof window.snowplowKW == 'function' ) {
			console.log('sending tracking code');
			window.snowplowKW( 'trackPageView' );
		}
	} catch ( err ) {
	}

	// Track Quantcast
	try {

		// need to reset the array containing the options previously sent
		// as quantcast does not send the same key twice.
		if (__qc && __qc.qpixelsent && __qc.qpixelsent.length > 0) {
			__qc.qpixelsent.length = 0;
		}
		// First Quantcast Tag
		_qoptions={
			qacct:""
		};

		quantserve();

	} catch(err) {}

	// Track Comscore unless it's a gallery and has been tracked
	if ( window.pmc.comscoreTracked && -1 === window.pmc.comscoreTracked.indexOf( document.location.href ) ) {
		try {
			setTimeout(function(){var url = "http" + (/^https:/.test(document.location.href) ? "s" : "") + "://beacon.scorecardresearch.com/scripts/beacon.dll" + "?c1=2&amp;c2=6035310&amp;c4=&amp;c7=" + escape(document.location.href) + "&amp;c8=" + escape(document.title) + "&amp;c9=" + escape(document.referrer) + "&amp;c10=" + escape(screen.width + 'x' + screen.height) + "&amp;rn=" + (new Date()).getTime();var i = new Image();i.src = url;}, 1);

			COMSCORE.beacon({c1:2,c2:"6035310",c4:""});

		} catch(err) {}
	}

	if (
	'undefined' !== typeof PARSELY &&
	'undefined' !== typeof PARSELY.beacon &&
	'function' === typeof PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView
) {
	PARSELY.beacon.trackPageView();
}
	/**
	* Track pageview end
	*/
}

			return pushState.apply(history, arguments);
			}
		})(window.history);

		// Trigger comscore beacon on change location.href
		window.onpopstate = history.onpushstate = function() {
			if ( typeof COMSCORE !== 'undefined' ) {
				setTimeout( function() {
					COMSCORE.beacon(comscore_vals);
				}, 1);
			}
		};
	</script>
